	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: dev/translation/generate_proof_files.phps');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('dev/translation/generate_proof_files.phps')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): dev/translation/generate_proof_files.phps');
	} else if (sha1_file('dev/translation/generate_proof_files.phps') != '163d4f4febeeae041c3fd1b4c7b34fa2cb94ed07') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): dev/translation/generate_proof_files.phps');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('dev/translation/generate_proof_files.phps', 0755)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of dev/translation/generate_proof_files.phps');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('dev/translation/generate_proof_files.phps') !== '163d4f4febeeae041c3fd1b4c7b34fa2cb94ed07') {
		if (@sha1_file('dev/translation/generate_proof_files.phps') !== 'd01f03011179b463ed84dc5a1ce9f0ed5fc96efe') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: dev/translation/generate_proof_files.phps');
			$tmp = pathinfo('dev/translation/generate_proof_files.phps');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('dev/translation/generate_proof_files.phps')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('dev/translation/generate_proof_files.phps', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('dev/translation/generate_proof_files.phps') !== '163d4f4febeeae041c3fd1b4c7b34fa2cb94ed07') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): dev/translation/generate_proof_files.phps');
		}
	}

if (!is_file('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps');
	writefile_2();
	if (!is_file('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps');
	} else if (sha1_file('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps') != '57132e932249e250c51bf4147f872dd9380a595c') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps', 0755)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps') !== '57132e932249e250c51bf4147f872dd9380a595c') {
		if (@sha1_file('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps') !== 'ac877d4f579f76f13d2ed500470209e7e881a2a3') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps');
			$tmp = pathinfo('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps') !== '57132e932249e250c51bf4147f872dd9380a595c') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: dev/translation/show_nontranslated_code.phps');
	writefile_3();
	if (!is_file('dev/translation/show_nontranslated_code.phps')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): dev/translation/show_nontranslated_code.phps');
	} else if (sha1_file('dev/translation/show_nontranslated_code.phps') != '7d7912d87099eb888f26c9e65e0f642cb97ae05c') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): dev/translation/show_nontranslated_code.phps');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('dev/translation/show_nontranslated_code.phps', 0755)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of dev/translation/show_nontranslated_code.phps');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('dev/translation/show_nontranslated_code.phps') !== '7d7912d87099eb888f26c9e65e0f642cb97ae05c') {
		if (@sha1_file('dev/translation/show_nontranslated_code.phps') !== '78fc0c73c024edd63f1c2367d604b37284315de9') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: dev/translation/show_nontranslated_code.phps');
			$tmp = pathinfo('dev/translation/show_nontranslated_code.phps');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('dev/translation/show_nontranslated_code.phps')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('dev/translation/show_nontranslated_code.phps', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('dev/translation/show_nontranslated_code.phps') !== '7d7912d87099eb888f26c9e65e0f642cb97ae05c') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): dev/translation/show_nontranslated_code.phps');

if (!is_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html');
	writefile_9();
	if (!is_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html');
	} else if (sha1_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html') != '7599f8479f0f2f2fd1211a7f6e71a4e8115ecdc9') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html') !== '7599f8479f0f2f2fd1211a7f6e71a4e8115ecdc9') {
		if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html') !== 'f24a8890a55e126feb211cc2bcee1ccf03571264') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html');
			$tmp = pathinfo('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_9();
		if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html') !== '7599f8479f0f2f2fd1211a7f6e71a4e8115ecdc9') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation$dede.html')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation$dede.html');
	writefile_10();
	if (!is_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation$dede.html')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation$dede.html');
	} else if (sha1_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation$dede.html') != '92ea712ded56d663f7fc6c758e1e72044a0c7fd3') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation$dede.html');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation$dede.html', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation$dede.html');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation$dede.html') !== '92ea712ded56d663f7fc6c758e1e72044a0c7fd3') {
		if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation$dede.html') !== '2a282e7f88496f30cd5b9bc0ddefa3e7e3752c8f') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation$dede.html');
			$tmp = pathinfo('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation$dede.html');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation$dede.html')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation$dede.html', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_10();
		if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation$dede.html') !== '92ea712ded56d663f7fc6c758e1e72044a0c7fd3') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation$dede.html');
		}
	}
}
